    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer13785364971582436791">The Well House III: The Redemption: The ultimate evil now roams the earth in a human body in order to set up his kingdom and rule the world. <br/><br/>The year is 2016, and Ben Carson has fallen into a deep depression because his son, Taylor, has been held hostage for more than a year and Ben is unable to save him. Disturbing dreams are back, which give Ben clues on how to defeat th</span>
  <span id="freeText13785364971582436791" style="display:none">The Well House III: The Redemption: The ultimate evil now roams the earth in a human body in order to set up his kingdom and rule the world. <br /><br />The year is 2016, and Ben Carson has fallen into a deep depression because his son, Taylor, has been held hostage for more than a year and Ben is unable to save him. Disturbing dreams are back, which give Ben clues on how to defeat the evil power. Familiar characters return to help Ben on his quest. Ben and his dog, together with his wife, Anne, and daughter, Molly, enter the well house, and descend into the underworld in an effort to save his son. A great wizard, a Basque priest, and his old friend, Claude Moran, also accompany Ben, together with other familiar characters. They encounter terrifying dreams, dangerous creatures, and demonic angels on several journeys through the underworld, where some lives are lost during the search for redemption. <br /><br />The Well House III: The Redemption is an exciting drama that is part fantasy, part reality and part parable. It is filled with fire, magic and mystical spells, and takes you on an amazing journey from the mountains high above Boulder Colorado to the depths of hell. It continues the exciting and unique story of a man's fight against the ultimate evil. Will Ben win the battle and gain redemption or will he, his family and friends be destroyed and the world ruled by evil? The answer can be found in the chalice, the stones, and the water. The story of Ben's fight is finally concluded...or is it?<br /><br />The Well House III: The Redemption is the third book in the series called The Well House Chronicles.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13785364971582436791" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3062128260?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Judith L." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Judith L." href="/user/show/103124330-judith-l">Judith L.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3062128260" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1826191836976944833">Wow! Another page turner from M. S. Matassa! I read the first two of "The Well House" series and was so anxious to read "The Redemption," the third installment of this amazing story of Ben Carson, a decent man fighting the ultimate evil to save his beloved family. This book has it all; fantasy, magic, mystical spells, enchantment, suspense, excitement, creepy creatures and danger galore! Unforgettable character? Elias Grippe, a strange little fellow who dropped out of the sky saying he was the g</span>
  <span id="freeText1826191836976944833" style="display:none">Wow! Another page turner from M. S. Matassa! I read the first two of "The Well House" series and was so anxious to read "The Redemption," the third installment of this amazing story of Ben Carson, a decent man fighting the ultimate evil to save his beloved family. This book has it all; fantasy, magic, mystical spells, enchantment, suspense, excitement, creepy creatures and danger galore! Unforgettable character? Elias Grippe, a strange little fellow who dropped out of the sky saying he was the great and wonderful unmatched wizard who was going to help Ben in his quest! And there is the deep love of the family and friends and Ben's special love for his dog, Sherman. The author describes the characters so vividly that I really cared about them in their frightening adventure into the depths of hell. My reading choices are usually mysteries, detective and court room drama. This was new for me and I'm so glad I tried something different. I am hooked on "The Well House Chronicles" and I hope Mr. Matassa comes out with another novel....soon! A must read!!</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText14601281570882879016" style="display:none">Get ready for the deepest journey into the Dark than ever before with the third book in The Well House series by MS Matassa. Just like the other two books in the series, it was really imaginative and so well written. When reading it you feel like you're immersed in the atmospheric land where Ben Carson takes on the forces of evil once again. Ben has his family behind him and the magical and mythical friends he has met along the way, but will it be enough?<br /><br />Another great piece of fiction that is fast-paced and full of interesting and empathetic characters. The plot kept me guessing from start to finish and like the other two books in the series, really unique and interesting.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText17535758400675433909" style="display:none">I have read the first two novels in the Well House series so was really looking forward to making a start on this one. I didn't think that Matassa could top the second book, however, I don't mind admitting that I was wrong! I found this to be a fabulous read and dare I say even better than the first two in the series. Again a fast paced book that kept me totally engrossed the entire way through, extremely well written with amazingly captivating characters. Well done Matassa for exceeding my expectations, I will look forward to reading more books by this author and I am in no doubt about recommending this book to friends and family, however I would also recommend reading the first two books in the series to ensure you get full enjoyment.</span>

<div id="review_3106948944" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3106948944" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3106948944?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3106948944" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7875340135127218776">‘I will not give p this life. No one will defeat me.’<br/><br/>Colorado author Michael S. Matassa earned his degrees from Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law and is an attorney and Municipal Court Judge in Arvada, Colorado. THE WELL HOUSE was his debut novel though he has also written several short stories and a screenplay. The Well House Chronicles continued with THE REVENGE and now THE REDEMPTION is Volume III. He states he discovered the well house in the late summer of</span>
  <span id="freeText7875340135127218776" style="display:none">‘I will not give p this life. No one will defeat me.’<br /><br />Colorado author Michael S. Matassa earned his degrees from Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law and is an attorney and Municipal Court Judge in Arvada, Colorado. THE WELL HOUSE was his debut novel though he has also written several short stories and a screenplay. The Well House Chronicles continued with THE REVENGE and now THE REDEMPTION is Volume III. He states he discovered the well house in the late summer of 1994, standing by a field of corn on a small farm just south of Brighton Colorado, where it still stands today. His nom de plume is M.S. Matassa.<br /><br />The author’s skillful scene painting provides the curtain raiser for this novel and a brisk recap of the first two novels in the series – ‘In the summer of 1998, Ben Carson faced the ultimate evil – and won. Once his wife, Anna, recovered form the coma, she gave birth to a daughter named Molly. The family continued to live in the same A-frame house in the mountains near Boulder, Colorado and life was peaceful and fulfilling. Ben became a successful writer, and Anne volunteered time at a Boulder homeless shelter, counseling residents with mental disabilities. Their son, Taylor, got a job in Denver at a television station as a reporter and married his longtime love, Jenny…’ The summary of events pulses on as the new stage of adventure unveils. <br /><br />The saga continues as condensed in the author’s synopsis – ‘The ultimate evil now roams the earth in a human body in order to set up his kingdom and rule the world. The year is 2016, and Ben Carson has fallen into a deep depression because his son, Taylor, has been held hostage for more than a year and Ben is unable to save him. Disturbing dreams are back, which give Ben clues on how to defeat the evil power. Familiar characters return to help Ben on his quest. Ben and his dog, together with his wife, Anne, and daughter, Molly, enter the well house, and descend into the underworld in an effort to save his son. A great wizard, a Basque priest, and his old friend, Claude Moran, also accompany Ben, together with other familiar characters. They encounter terrifying dreams, dangerous creatures, and demonic angels on several journeys through the underworld, where some lives are lost during the search for redemption. Will Ben win the battle and gain redemption or will he, his family and friends be destroyed and the world ruled by evil? The answer can be found in the chalice, the stones, and the water. The story of Ben's fight is finally concluded...or is it?’<br /><br />THE WELL HOUSE CHRONICLES is one of the most satisfying paranormal fantasies before the public at this time. While reading the entire series is recommended, THE REDEMPTION is so well written that it stands alone as a fine novel. Recommended.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7875340135127218776" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4473445797335393147">The Well House III: The Redemption continues the eerie fight between Satan and Ben Carson. M.S. Matassa begins with Ben depressed with how his last battle with Satan ended and the price he paid with his family. Has he lost faith in God and is willing to give into the Devil? The thrill of the fight is felt through the pages as Jack St. Louis, aka Satan, begins to have nightmares. Ben Carson is ready to take back what is his and the power felt through the nightmares puts Satan on edge. It is a rac</span>
  <span id="freeText4473445797335393147" style="display:none">The Well House III: The Redemption continues the eerie fight between Satan and Ben Carson. M.S. Matassa begins with Ben depressed with how his last battle with Satan ended and the price he paid with his family. Has he lost faith in God and is willing to give into the Devil? The thrill of the fight is felt through the pages as Jack St. Louis, aka Satan, begins to have nightmares. Ben Carson is ready to take back what is his and the power felt through the nightmares puts Satan on edge. It is a race to see who wins Taylor as both Lucifer and Ben puts their plans into action. <br /><br />I love the suspense and action M.S. Matassa weaves within his novels. The Well House III: The Redemption is a book you cannot put down as the forces of evil faces the love of a father and his friends of various spiritual skills. Nightmares warn the characters of events about to happen and when they learn to take these dreams seriously it allows them to form plans. You can feel the energy from the characters and the well-written precision from the author, which gives this book an edge. I highly recommend this series and have enjoyed thrill this novel emits. <br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d5Dhs/63aVMtw7YlxW2dPkcp2nnBoElyayKGl0B3exyrCn5/Ku6V/yct1yZU+/fQflsE/kia+BJExQXS4e7hQA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ndl6viKAV01ivIxowJvGC2TuaW+RvKlfGryOetBI69JBQ+Vy9tmr4WhS7WtRDazlXZy36BiGGD81Ww0/cdFxjg==')})
  }
//]]>

Then a visit to Africa, and especially to Tanzania, reawakens the drumbeats and dancing that she carries in her soul. On her return home, she teaches Swahili and African Studies, performs African dance at schools, and creates Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout based on African dance. She both finds and creates the family she longed for as a child and connects with her unknown background. The first book of the trilogy, Africa’s Child, was released in 2016. <span id="freeTextContainer14208391828821970413">Michael S. Matassa is the author of The Well House, his first novel and several short stories. He was born in Dallas, Texas and now lives in Arvada, Colorado. Mr. Matassa is an attorney and a Municipal Court Judge. He attended Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law in Boulder, Colorado.<br/><br/>Mr. Matassa has finished a screenplay based on The Well House and is presently work</span>
  <span id="freeText14208391828821970413" style="display:none">Michael S. Matassa is the author of The Well House, his first novel and several short stories. He was born in Dallas, Texas and now lives in Arvada, Colorado. Mr. Matassa is an attorney and a Municipal Court Judge. He attended Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law in Boulder, Colorado.<br /><br />Mr. Matassa has finished a screenplay based on The Well House and is presently working on a two sequels to The Well House. He writes under the pen name of <br />M. S. Matassa.</span>
